[1mNAME[0m[m
       man - an interface to the system reference manuals[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mman [22m[[4mman[24m [4moptions[24m] [[[4msection[24m] [4mpage[24m ...] ...[m
       [1mman -k [22m[[4mapropos[24m [4moptions[24m] [4mregexp[24m ...[m
       [1mman -K [22m[[4mman[24m [4moptions[24m] [[4msection[24m] [4mterm[24m ...[m
       [1mman -f [22m[[4mwhatis[24m [4moptions[24m] [4mpage[24m ...[m
       [1mman -l [22m[[4mman[24m [4moptions[24m] [4mfile[24m ...[m
       [1mman -w[22m|[1m-W [22m[[4mman[24m [4moptions[24m] [4mpage[24m ...[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       [1mman  [22mis  the system's manual pager.  Each [4mpage[24m argument given to [1mman [22mis[m
       normally the name of a program, utility or function.  The  [4mmanual[24m  [4mpage[0m[m
       associated with each of these arguments is then found and displayed.  A[m
       [4msection[24m,  if  provided, will direct [1mman [22mto look only in that [4msection[24m of[m
[7m Manual page man(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K       the manual.  The default action is to search in all  of  the  available[m
       [4msections[24m following a pre-defined order (see [1mDEFAULTS[22m), and to show only[m
       the first [4mpage[24m found, even if [4mpage[24m exists in several [4msections[24m.[m
[m
       The table below shows the [4msection[24m numbers of the manual followed by the[m
       types of pages they contain.[m
[m
       1   Executable programs or shell commands[m

[1mNAME[0m[m
       crypttab - static information about encrypted filesystems[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       The file /etc/crypttab contains descriptive information about encrypted[m
       devices. crypttab is only read by programs (e.g. [1mcryptdisks_start [22mand[m
       [1mcryptdisks_stop[22m), and not written; it is the duty of the system[m
       administrator to properly create and maintain this file. crypttab[m
       entries are treated sequentially, so their order matters (dependencies[m
       need to listed first).[m
[m
       Each encrypted device is described on a separate line. Fields on each[m
       line are separated by tabs or spaces. Lines starting with '#' are[m
       comments, and blank lines are ignored. Octal sequences \0[4mnum[24m within a[m
       field are decoded, which can be used for values containing spaces or[m
       special characters. A backslash which doesn't start an octal sequence[m
[7m Manual page crypttab(5) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       yields undefined behavior.[m
[7m Manual page crypttab(5) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page crypttab(5) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       The first field, [4mtarget[24m, describes the mapped device name. It must be a[m
[7m Manual page crypttab(5) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       plain filename without any directory components. A mapped device which[m
[7m Manual page crypttab(5) line 5 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       encrypts/decrypts data to/from the [4msource[24m [4mdevice[24m will be created at[m
[7m Manual page crypttab(5) line 6 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       /dev/mapper/target by [1mcryptsetup[22m.[m
[7m Manual page crypttab(5) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page crypttab(5) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       The second field, [4msource[24m [4mdevice[24m, describes either the block special[m
